For customers in Great Britain, WHG (International) Limited is licensed and regulated in Great Britain by the Gambling Commission under account number 39225. For customers located in Great Britain, Jersey, Northern Ireland and Gibraltar, WHG (International) Limited is further licensed by the Government of Gibraltar and regulated by the Gibraltar Gambling Commissioner. WHG (International) Limited is a registered I.B.A.S bookmaker. WHG (International) Limited is a wholly owned subsidiary of evoke PLC, a company registered in Gibraltar and listed on the London Stock Exchange.

 

For customers outside of Great Britain, Northern Ireland, Jersey and Gibraltar, this website is operated by William Hill Global PLC, a company registered in Malta with registration number C96298. For customers in the Republic of Ireland, this website is operated by William Hill Malta PLC, with company number C87591.

Both William Hill Malta PLC and William Hill Global PLC, are companies registered in Malta with registered offices at Tagliaferro Business Centre, Level 7, High Street, Sliema SLM 1549, Malta. Both respective companies hold the following gambling licences: For Malta MGA/CRP/121/2006-05 issued by the  Malta Gaming Authority  ("MGA") on 2nd November 2020 and valid until 19th March 2028; for the Republic of Ireland the Game Type approved is Type 1, 2, and 3, and license number 1016824 issued by the Irish Revenue Commissioner.

Underage gambling is an offence. Gaming can be harmful if it is not controlled. William Hill is committed to helping you to gamble safely. For more information on the tools available to help to keep you safe please visit our Safer Gambling page.

For customers in Great Britain, WHG (International) Limited is licensed and regulated in Great Britain by the Gambling Commission under account number 39225. For customers located in Great Britain, Jersey, Northern Ireland and Gibraltar, WHG (International) Limited is further licensed by the Government of Gibraltar and regulated by the Gibraltar Gambling Commissioner. WHG (International) Limited is a registered I.B.A.S bookmaker. WHG (International) Limited is a wholly owned subsidiary of evoke PLC, a company registered in Gibraltar and listed on the London Stock Exchange.

 

For customers outside of Great Britain, Northern Ireland, Jersey and Gibraltar, this website is operated by William Hill Global PLC, a company registered in Malta with registration number C96298. For customers in the Republic of Ireland, this website is operated by William Hill Malta PLC, with company number C87591.

Both William Hill Malta PLC and William Hill Global PLC, are companies registered in Malta with registered offices at Tagliaferro Business Centre, Level 7, High Street, Sliema SLM 1549, Malta. Both respective companies hold the following gambling licences: For Malta MGA/CRP/121/2006-05 issued by the  Malta Gaming Authority  ("MGA") on 2nd November 2020 and valid until 19th March 2028; for the Republic of Ireland the Game Type approved is Type 1, 2, and 3, and license number 1016824 issued by the Irish Revenue Commissioner.

Underage gambling is an offence. Gaming can be harmful if it is not controlled. William Hill is committed to helping you to gamble safely. For more information on the tools available to help to keep you safe please visit our Safer Gambling page.

For customers in Great Britain, WHG (International) Limited is licensed and regulated in Great Britain by the Gambling Commission under account number 39225. For customers located in Great Britain, Jersey, Northern Ireland and Gibraltar, WHG (International) Limited is further licensed by the Government of Gibraltar and regulated by the Gibraltar Gambling Commissioner. WHG (International) Limited is a registered I.B.A.S bookmaker. WHG (International) Limited is a wholly owned subsidiary of evoke PLC, a company registered in Gibraltar and listed on the London Stock Exchange.

 

For customers outside of Great Britain, Northern Ireland, Jersey and Gibraltar, this website is operated by William Hill Global PLC, a company registered in Malta with registration number C96298. For customers in the Republic of Ireland, this website is operated by William Hill Malta PLC, with company number C87591.

Both William Hill Malta PLC and William Hill Global PLC, are companies registered in Malta with registered offices at Tagliaferro Business Centre, Level 7, High Street, Sliema SLM 1549, Malta. Both respective companies hold the following gambling licences: For Malta MGA/CRP/121/2006-05 issued by the  Malta Gaming Authority  ("MGA") on 2nd November 2020 and valid until 19th March 2028; for the Republic of Ireland the Game Type approved is Type 1, 2, and 3, and license number 1016824 issued by the Irish Revenue Commissioner.

Underage gambling is an offence. Gaming can be harmful if it is not controlled. William Hill is committed to helping you to gamble safely. For more information on the tools available to help to keep you safe please visit our Safer Gambling page.
